  * grade_story_103.txt (grade=7.0)
    Cohesion emerges from its commitment to surreal symbolism over conventional realism. Assigned elements are deployed with obsessive care, though the knight’s interiority remains secondary to atmosphere. The brief length works as a constraint, demanding brevity but sacrificing deeper exploration of motifs. Leaves impressionistic echoes of sacrifice and pattern-seeking, if not emotional immersion.

  * grade_story_100.txt (grade=5.0)
    Cohesive as a linguistic puzzle box, but sacrifices emotional urgency for conceptual density; too esoteric for immediate publishability.

  * grade_story_1.txt (grade=9.3)
